NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING CHANGE
OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES WILL
REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
S. Nasar was born as a male child to S. Saliem (late) on 3rd July 1990, residing at No. 74/10, Jayam Illam,
A.R. Thoppu 1st Street, Vasantha Nagar, Madurai-625 003. After an elaborate Sexual Reassignment Surgery, She has
been living as a female [Reference to Dr. P. Raja M.S., M.Ch., (Uro) Lecturer., Department of Uro., Rajaji Government
Hospital at Madurai-625 004], The through Clinical Examination after the plant surgery shows that I could be treated as
female and S. NASAR shall henceforth be known as S. SWAPNA.

Madurai,
4th June 2012.

S. NASAR.

V. Gulasekar, was born as male child to A. Vengatachalam on 29th July 1968, residing at Old No. 12C,
New No. 32, Singarapettai, Salem-636 002. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery, She has been living as a
female (Refer Dr. C. Janaki, M.B.B.S., M.S. Reg. No. 37050 Civil Assistant Surgeon, Government Head Quarters Hospital,
Erode) The through clinical examination under Dr. C. Janaki M.B.B.S., M.S., shows that I could be treated as female
V. Gulasekar shall be known as V. Vimala.

Salem,
8th June 2012.

V. GULASEKAR.
